Here’s how to make the most of it.</p> <h2 id="-learning-strategies"><a class="header" href="#-learning-strategies">🎯 Learning Strategies</a></h2> <h3 id="for-beginners"><a class="header" href="#for-beginners">For Beginners</a></h3> <ol> <li><strong>Follow the Roadmap</strong>: Start with the <a href="#12-month-developer-roadmap">Roadmap</a> and follow the 12-month plan</li> <li><strong>Sequential Learning</strong>: Complete sections in order - each builds on previous knowledge</li> <li><strong>Hands-On Practice</strong>: Code along with every example</li> <li><strong>Project-Based Learning</strong>: Build the suggested projects after each section</li> </ol> <h3 id="for-intermediate-developers"><a class="header" href="#for-intermediate-developers">For Intermediate Developers</a></h3> <ol> <li><strong>Modular Learning</strong>: Jump to sections that fill your knowledge gaps</li> <li><strong>Cross-Reference</strong>: Connect concepts across different technologies</li> <li><strong>Advanced Projects</strong>: Focus on the complex project implementations</li> <li><strong>Best Practices</strong>: Pay attention to architectural patterns and design decisions</li> </ol> <h3 id="for-advanced-developers"><a class="header" href="#for-advanced-developers">For Advanced Developers</a></h3> <ol> <li><strong>Reference Guide</strong>: Use as a quick reference for implementations</li> <li><strong>System Design</strong>: Study the architecture decisions in project sections</li> <li><strong>Career Strategies</strong>: Implement the freelancing and branding techniques</li> <li><strong>Teaching</strong>: Use concepts to mentor junior developers</li> </ol> <h2 id="-reading-guidelines"><a class="header" href="#-reading-guidelines">📖 Reading Guidelines</a></h2> <h3 id="code-examples"><a class="header" href="#code-examples">Code Examples</a></h3> <ul> <li><strong>Read First</strong>: Understand the concept before coding</li> <li><strong>Type It Out</strong>: Don’t copy-paste - type every line</li> <li><strong>Experiment</strong>: Modify examples to see what happens</li> <li><strong>Break It</strong>: Try to break the code and fix it</li> </ul> <h3 id="project-sections"><a class="header" href="#project-sections">Project Sections</a></h3> <p>Each project includes:</p> <ul> <li><strong>Overview</strong>: What we’re building and why</li> <li><strong>Features</strong>: Complete feature list</li> <li><strong>Tech Stack</strong>: Technologies used</li> <li><strong>Folder Structure</strong>: Project organization</li> <li><strong>Implementation</strong>: Step-by-step guide</li> <li><strong>Deployment</strong>: How to go live</li> </ul> <h3 id="diagrams-and-visuals"><a class="header" href="#diagrams-and-visuals">Diagrams and Visuals</a></h3> <ul> <li><strong>Study Carefully</strong>: Visual aids show complex concepts</li> <li><strong>Recreate</strong>: Draw your own versions to reinforce learning</li> <li><strong>Reference</strong>: Come back when implementing similar patterns</li> </ul> <h2 id="-practical-tips"><a class="header" href="#-practical-tips">🛠️ Practical Tips</a></h2> <h3 id="environment-setup"><a class="header" href="#environment-setup">Environment Setup</a></h3> <ol> <li><strong>Consistent Setup</strong>: Use the same tools and versions as shown</li> <li><strong>Version Control</strong>: Git every project from day one</li> <li><strong>Documentation</strong>: Keep your own notes and code comments</li> <li><strong>Backup</strong>: Use GitHub or similar for all projects</li> </ol> <h3 id="learning-schedule"><a class="header" href="#learning-schedule">Learning Schedule</a></h3> <h4 id="daily-routine-1-2-hours"><a class="header" id="weekly-schedule"><a class="header" href="#weekly-schedule">Weekly Schedule</a></h4> <ul> <li>Monday-Wednesday: New content</li> <li>Thursday: Project work</li> <li>Friday: Review and debugging</li> <li>Weekend: Personal projects and exploration</li> </ul> <h3 id="common-pitfalls-to-avoid"><a class="header" href="#common-pitfalls-to-avoid">Common Pitfalls to Avoid</a></h3> <p>❌ <strong>Don’t</strong>:</p> <ul> <li>Skip fundamentals</li> <li>Copy-paste without understanding</li> <li>Jump between topics randomly</li> <li>Ignore error messages</li> <li>Skip testing</li> </ul> <p>✅ <strong>Do</strong>:</p> <ul> <li>Master basics first</li> <li>Type every line of code</li> <li>Follow the learning path</li> <li>Debug thoroughly</li> <li>Test everything</li> </ul> <h2 Stay consistent, stay curious, and keep building! 🚀</p> <div style="break-before: page; page-break-before: always;"></div> <h1 id="12-month-developer-roadmap"><a class="header" href="#12-month-developer-roadmap">12-Month Developer Roadmap</a></h1> <p>This roadmap takes you from complete beginner to job-ready full-stack developer with AI integration skills.</p> <h2 id="-month-by-month-breakdown"><a class="header" href="#-month-by-month-breakdown">📅 Month-by-Month Breakdown</a></h2> <h3 id="months-1-3-foundation-fundamentals"><a class="header" href="#months-1-3-foundation-fundamentals">Months 1-3: Foundation Fundamentals</a></h3> <p><strong>Goal</strong>: Build strong programming fundamentals</p> <h4 id="month-1-web-basics"><a class="header" href="#month-1-web-basics">Month 1: Web Basics</a></h4> <ul> <li><strong>HTML5</strong>: Semantic markup, forms, accessibility</li> <li><strong>CSS3</strong>: Layouts, Flexbox, Grid, responsive design</li> <li><strong>JavaScript Basics</strong>: Variables, functions, DOM manipulation</li> <li><strong>Project</strong>: Personal portfolio website</li> <li><strong>Skills</strong>: Structure web pages, style professionally, add interactivity</li> </ul> <h4 id="month-2-javascript-mastery"><a class="header" href="#month-2-javascript-mastery">Month 2: JavaScript Mastery</a></h4> <ul> <li><strong>Advanced JS</strong>: Arrays, objects, async/await, promises</li> <li><strong>ES6+ Features</strong>: Destructuring, spread, modules</li> <li><strong>DOM &amp; Events</strong>: Event handling, form validation</li> <li><strong>Project</strong>: Interactive web application</li> <li><strong>Skills</strong>: Write clean JavaScript, handle async operations</li> </ul> <h4 id="month-3-version-control--tools"><a class="header" href="#month-3-version-control--tools">Month 3: Version Control &amp; Tools</a></h4> <ul> <li><strong>Git &amp; GitHub</strong>: Branching, merging, pull requests</li> <li><strong>Terminal Basics</strong>: Command line operations</li> <li><strong>Code Quality</strong>: Linting, formatting, debugging</li> <li><strong>Project</strong>: Open source contribution</li> <li><strong>Skills</strong>: Professional development workflow</li> </ul> <h3 id="months-4-6-mobile-development-with-react-native"><a class="header" href="#months-4-6-mobile-development-with-react-native">Months 4-6: Mobile Development with React Native</a></h3> <p><strong>Goal</strong>: Build cross-platform mobile applications</p> <h4 id="month-4-react-native-fundamentals"><a class="header" href="#month-4-react-native-fundamentals">Month 4: React Native Fundamentals</a></h4> <ul> <li><strong>Setup</strong>: Environment, Expo vs CLI</li> <li><strong>Components</strong>: Core components, custom components</li> <li><strong>Styling</strong>: StyleSheet, responsive design</li> <li><strong>Project</strong>: Simple calculator app</li> <li><strong>Skills</strong>: Build basic mobile interfaces</li> </ul> <h4 id="month-5-advanced-react-native"><a class="header" href="#month-5-advanced-react-native">Month 5: Advanced React Native</a></h4> <ul> <li><strong>Navigation</strong>: React Navigation setup</li> <li><strong>State Management</strong>: Context API, Redux basics</li> <li><strong>API Integration</strong>: Fetch, Axios, async operations</li> <li><strong>Project</strong>: Weather app with API integration</li> <li><strong>Skills</strong>: Complex app architecture, data flow</li> </ul> <h4 id="month-6-production-react-native"><a class="header" href="#month-6-production-react-native">Month 6: Production React Native</a></h4> <ul> <li><strong>Storage</strong>: AsyncStorage, secure storage</li> <li><strong>Performance</strong>: Optimization techniques</li> <li><strong>Testing</strong>: Jest, React Native Testing Library</li> <li><strong>Project</strong>: Full-featured mobile app</li> <li><strong>Skills</strong>: Production-ready mobile development</li> </ul> <h3 id="months-7-9-full-stack-web-development"><a class="header" href="#months-7-9-full-stack-web-development">Months 7-9: Full-Stack Web Development</a></h3> <p><strong>Goal</strong>: Build complete web applications</p> <h4 id="month-7-modern-frontend"><a class="header" href="#month-7-modern-frontend">Month 7: Modern Frontend</a></h4> <ul> <li><strong>React Fundamentals</strong>: Components, hooks, state</li> <li><strong>Next.js</strong>: Routing, SSR, API routes</li> <li><strong>UI/UX</strong>: Design systems, accessibility</li> <li><strong>Project</strong>: Modern web application</li> <li><strong>Skills</strong>: Professional frontend development</li> </ul> <h4 id="month-8-backend-development"><a class="header" href="#month-8-backend-development">Month 8: Backend Development</a></h4> <ul> <li><strong>Node.js</strong>: Express, middleware, routing</li> <li><strong>APIs</strong>: REST, GraphQL basics</li> <li><strong>Authentication</strong>: JWT, OAuth, sessions</li> <li><strong>Project</strong>: Complete API backend</li> <li><strong>Skills</strong>: Server-side development, security</li> </ul> <h4 id="month-9-database--deployment"><a class="header" href="#month-9-database--deployment">Month 9: Database &amp; Deployment</a></h4> <ul> <li><strong>MongoDB</strong>: Schema design, CRUD operations</li> <li><strong>Full Integration</strong>: Connect frontend to backend</li> <li><strong>Deployment</strong>: Vercel, Render, environment management</li> <li><strong>Project</strong>: Deployed full-stack application</li> <li><strong>Skills</strong>: End-to-end development</li> </ul> <h3 id="months-10-12-ai-integration--career"><a class="header" href="#months-10-12-ai-integration--career">Months 10-12: AI Integration &amp; Career</a></h3> <p><strong>Goal</strong>: Build AI-powered applications and launch career</p> <h4 id="month-10-ai-development"><a class="header" href="#month-10-ai-development">Month 10: AI Development</a></h4> <ul> <li><strong>Prompt Engineering</strong>: Effective AI prompting</li> <li><strong>ChatGPT API</strong>: Integration, best practices</li> <li><strong>AI Safety</strong>: Ethics, limitations, security</li> <li><strong>Project</strong>: AI-powered application</li> <li><strong>Skills</strong>: Modern AI integration</li> </ul> <h4 id="month-11-advanced-projects"><a class="header" href="#month-11-advanced-projects">Month 11: Advanced Projects</a></h4> <ul> <li><strong>System Design</strong>: Architecture patterns</li> <li><strong>Testing</strong>: Unit, integration, E2E testing</li> <li><strong>Performance</strong>: Optimization, monitoring</li> <li><strong>Project</strong>: Portfolio-worthy application</li> <li><strong>Skills</strong>: Production-grade development</li> </ul> <h4 id="month-12-career-launch"><a class="header" href="#month-12-career-launch">Month 12: Career Launch</a></h4> <ul> <li><strong>Portfolio</strong>: Curate and showcase projects</li> <li><strong>Freelancing</strong>: Client acquisition, pricing</li> <li><strong>Interview Prep</strong>: Technical and behavioral</li> <li><strong>Personal Branding</strong>: Online presence</li> <li><strong>Skills</strong>: Professional career development</li> </ul> <h2 id="-key-milestones"><a class="header" href="#-key-milestones">🎯 Key Milestones</a></h2> <h3 id="milestone-1-foundation-complete-month-3"><a class="header" professionally</p> <h3 id="milestone-2-mobile-developer-month-6"><a class="header" href="#milestone-2-mobile-developer-month-6">Milestone 2: Mobile Developer (Month 6)</a></h3> <p>✅ Can build cross-platform mobile apps<br>✅ Understand mobile app architecture<br>✅ Can deploy to app stores</p> <h3 id="milestone-3-full-stack-developer-month-9"><a class="header" href="#milestone-3-full-stack-developer-month-9">Milestone 3: Full-Stack Developer (Month 9)</a></h3> <p>✅ Can build complete web applications<br>✅ Understand database design<br>✅ Can deploy production applications</p> <h3 id="milestone-4-ai-enhanced-developer-month-12"><a class="header" href="#milestone-4-ai-enhanced-developer-month-12">Milestone 4: AI-Enhanced Developer (Month 12)</a></h3> <p>✅ Can integrate AI into applications<br>✅ Have professional portfolio<br>✅ Ready for career opportunities</p> <h2 id="-weekly-time-commitment"><a class="header" <li><strong>Weekdays</strong>: 1-2 hours daily</li> <li><strong>Weekends</strong>: 3-4 hours total</li> <li><strong>Total</strong>: 8-12 hours per week</li> </ul> <h3 id="daily-breakdown"><a class="header" href="#daily-breakdown">Daily Breakdown</a></h3> <ul> <li><strong>30 min</strong>: Learning new concepts</li> <li><strong>45 min</strong>: Hands-on coding</li> <li><strong>15 min</strong>: Review and documentation</li> </ul> <h2 id="-technology-stack-timeline"><a class="header" href="#-technology-stack-timeline">🛠️ Technology Stack Timeline</a></h2> <pre><code class="language-mermaid">graph TD A[HTML/CSS/JS] --&gt; B[Git/GitHub] B --&gt; C[React Native] C --&gt; D[React/Next.js] D --&gt; E[Node.js/Express] E --&gt; F[MongoDB] F --&gt; G[AI Integration] G --&gt; H[Production Deployment] </code></pre> <h2 id="-skill-progression"><a class="header" href="#-skill-progression">📈 Skill Progression</a></h2> <h3 id="technical-skills-1"><a class="header" href="#technical-skills-1">Technical Skills</a></h3> <ol> <li><strong>Frontend</strong>: HTML → CSS → JavaScript → React → Next.js</li> <li><strong>Mobile</strong>: React Native → Navigation → State → Testing</li> <li><strong>Backend</strong>: Node.js → Express → APIs → Database</li> <li><strong>AI</strong>: Prompting → Integration → Applications → Ethics</li> </ol> <h3 id="professional-skills-1"><a class="header" href="#professional-skills-1">Professional Skills</a></h3> <ol> <li><strong>Development</strong>: Git → Testing → Debugging → Documentation</li> <li><strong>Architecture</strong>: Components → State → Performance → Security</li> <li><strong>Career</strong>: Portfolio → Networking → Freelancing → Branding</li> </ol> <h2 id="-success-indicators"><a class="header" href="#-success-indicators">🎯 Success Indicators</a></h2> <h3 id="monthly-checkpoints"><a class="header" href="#monthly-checkpoints">Monthly </ul> <h3 id="if-youre-ahead"><a class="header" href="#if-youre-ahead">If You’re Ahead</a></h3> <ul> <li>Explore advanced topics</li> <li>Build additional projects</li> <li>Start freelancing with basic skills</li> <li>Contribute to open source</li> </ul> <h3 id="if-youre-stuck"><a class="header" href="#if-youre-stuck">If You’re Stuck</a></h3> <ul> <li>Review previous months’ content</li> <li>Join developer communities</li> <li>Find a mentor or study partner</li> <li>Take breaks, avoid burnout</li> </ul> <hr> <p><strong>Remember</strong>: This is a guide, not a rigid rulebook. Adjust based on your learning style, goals, and available time. The key is consistency and practical application! 🚀</p> <div style="break-before: page; page-break-before: always;"></div> <h1 id="introduction-to-react-native"><a class="header" href="#introduction-to-react-native">Introduction to React Native</a></h1> <p>React Native is a framework for building native mobile apps using JavaScript and React. It lets you write real, natively rendered mobile applications for iOS and Android - all from a single codebase.</p> <h2 id="-what-is-react-native"><a class="header" href="#-what-is-react-native">🎯 What is React Native?</a></h2> <p>React Native is:</p> <ul> <li><strong>Cross-platform</strong>: One codebase for iOS and Android</li> <li><strong>Native Performance</strong>: Uses actual native UI components</li> <li><strong>JavaScript-based</strong>: Use your web development skills</li> <li><strong>React-powered</strong>: Component-based architecture</li> <li><strong>Facebook-backed</strong>: Strong community and support</li> </ul> <h2 id="-why-react-native"><a class="header" href="#-why-react-native">🚀 Why React Native?</a></h2> <h3 id="advantages"><a class="header" href="#advantages">Advantages</a></h3> <ul> <li><strong>Single Codebase</strong>: Write once, deploy everywhere</li> <li><strong>Fast Development</strong>: Hot reloading, instant feedback</li> <li><strong>Native Feel</strong>: Real native UI components</li> <li><strong>Large Community</strong>: Extensive libraries and support</li> <li><strong>Cost Effective</strong>: Half the development cost of native apps</li> </ul> <h3 id="use-cases"><a class="header" href="#use-cases">Use Cases</a></h3> <ul> <li>Startups and MVPs</li> <li>Content-driven apps</li> <li>Social applications</li> <li>E-commerce mobile apps</li> <li>Business productivity apps</li> </ul> <h2 id="-core-concepts"><a class="header" href="#-core-concepts">🛠️ Core Concepts</a></h2> <h3 id="components"><a class="header" href="#components">Components</a></h3> <p>React Native uses the same component concepts as React:</p> <pre><code class="language-javascript">import React from 'react'; import { View, Text, StyleSheet } from 'react-native'; const WelcomeScreen = () =&gt; { return ( &lt;View style={styles.container}&gt; &lt;Text style={styles.title}&gt;Welcome to React Native!&lt;/Text&gt; &lt;/View&gt; ); }; const styles = StyleSheet.create({ container: { flex: 1, justifyContent: 'center', alignItems: 'center', }, title: { fontSize: 24, fontWeight: 'bold', }, }); export default WelcomeScreen; </code></pre> <h3 id="core-components"><a class="header" href="#core-components">Core Components</a></h3> <ul> <li><strong>View</strong>: Container component (like div in web)</li> <li><strong>Text</strong>: Text display component</li> <li><strong>Image</strong>: Image display component</li> <li><strong>ScrollView</strong>: Scrollable container</li> <li><strong>TextInput</strong>: User input field</li> <li><strong>TouchableOpacity</strong>: Pressable button</li> <li><strong>FlatList</strong>: Efficient list rendering</li> </ul> <h2 id="-architecture"><a class="header" href="#-architecture">🏗️ Architecture</a></h2> <h3 id="react-native-bridge"><a class="header" href="#react-native-bridge">React Native Bridge</a></h3> <p>React Native uses a bridge to communicate between JavaScript and native code:</p> <pre><code class="language-text">JavaScript Code → React Native Bridge → Native Modules → Native UI </code></pre> <h3 id="thread-model"><a class="header" href="#thread-model">Thread Model</a></h3> <ul> <li><strong>UI Thread</strong>: Renders native UI components</li> <li><strong>JavaScript Thread</strong>: Runs your JavaScript code</li> <li><strong>Shadow Thread</strong>: Calculates layouts</li> </ul> <h2 id="-setup-options"><a class="header" href="#-setup-options">📱 Setup Options</a></h2> <h3 id="1-expo-recommended-for-beginners"><a class="header" href="#1-expo-recommended-for-beginners">1. Expo (Recommended for Beginners)</a></h3> <p>Expo is a framework and platform for universal React applications.</p> <p><strong>Advantages:</strong></p> <ul> <li>No native code required</li> <li>Easy setup and deployment</li> <li>Built-in services (push notifications, OTA updates)</li> <li>Great for beginners</li> </ul> <p><strong>Installation:</strong></p> <pre><code class="language-bash">npm install -g expo-cli expo init my-app cd my-app npm start </code></pre> <h3 id="2-react-native-cli"><a class="header" href="#2-react-native-cli">2. React Native CLI</a></h3> <p>For more control and native module access.</p> <p><strong>Advantages:</strong></p> <ul> <li>Full control over native code</li> <li>Access to any native module</li> <li>Better for complex apps</li> </ul> <p><strong>Installation:</strong></p> <pre><code class="language-bash">npx react-native init MyApp cd MyApp npx react-native run-android # or run-ios </code></pre> <h2 id="-styling-in-react-native"><a class="header" href="#-styling-in-react-native">🎨 Styling in React Native</a></h2> <h3 id="stylesheet-api"><a class="header" href="#stylesheet-api">StyleSheet API</a></h3> <p>React Native uses JavaScript-based styling:</p> <pre><code class="language-javascript">import { StyleSheet } from 'react-native'; const styles = StyleSheet.create({ container: { flex: 1, backgroundColor: '#fff', padding: 20, }, button: { backgroundColor: '#007AFF', padding: 15, borderRadius: 8, alignItems: 'center', }, buttonText: { color: '#fff', fontSize: 16, fontWeight: 'bold', }, }); </code></pre> <h3 id="flexbox-layout"><a class="header" href="#flexbox-layout">Flexbox Layout</a></h3> <p>React Native uses Flexbox for layout (default direction is column):</p> <pre><code class="language-javascript">const styles = StyleSheet.create({ row: { flexDirection: 'row', // Horizontal layout justifyContent: 'center', // Horizontal alignment alignItems: 'center', // Vertical alignment }, column: { flexDirection: 'column', // Vertical layout (default) justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'stretch', }, }); </code></pre> <h2 id="-development-workflow"><a class="header" href="#-development-workflow">🔄 Development Workflow</a></h2> <h3 id="hot-reloading"><a class="header" href="#hot-reloading">Hot Reloading</a></h3> <ul> <li><strong>Fast Refresh</strong>: Instantly see changes</li> <li><strong>State Preservation</strong>: Component state maintained during reload</li> <li><strong>Error Recovery</strong>: Automatic recovery from errors</li> </ul> <h3 id="debugging-tools"><a class="header" href="#debugging-tools">Debugging Tools</a></h3> <ul> <li><strong>React Native Debugger</strong>: Comprehensive debugging</li> <li><strong>Flipper</strong>: Extensible mobile app debugger</li> <li><strong>Console Logs</strong>: Built-in logging</li> <li><strong>Remote Debugging</strong>: Chrome DevTools integration</li> </ul> <h2 id="-essential-libraries"><a class="header" href="#-essential-libraries">📦 Essential Libraries</a></h2> <h3 id="navigation"><a class="header" href="#navigation">Navigation</a></h3> <pre><code class="language-bash">npm install @react-navigation/native @react-navigation/stack npm install react-native-screens react-native-safe-area-context </code></pre> <h3 id="state-management"><a class="header" href="#state-management">State Management</a></h3> <pre><code class="language-bash">npm install @reduxjs/toolkit react-redux # or npm install @apollo/client graphql # for GraphQL </code></pre> <h3 id="ui-components"><a class="header" href="#ui-components">UI Components</a></h3> <pre><code class="language-bash">npm install react-native-elements npm install react-native-vector-icons </code></pre> <h3 id="utilities"><a class="header" href="#utilities">Utilities</a></h3> <pre><code class="language-bash">npm install react-native-async-storage npm install react-native-device-info npm install react-native-permissions </code></pre> <h2 id="-first-project-ideas"><a class="header" href="#-first-project-ideas">🎯 First Project Ideas</a></h2> <h3 id="beginner-projects"><a class="header" href="#beginner-projects">Beginner Projects</a></h3> <ol> <li><strong>Calculator App</strong>: Basic arithmetic operations</li> <li><strong>Todo List</strong>: CRUD operations with local storage</li> <li><strong>Weather App</strong>: API integration and data display</li> <li><strong>Recipe App</strong>: Search and display recipes</li> </ol> <h3 id="intermediate-projects"><a class="header" href="#intermediate-projects">Intermediate Projects</a></h3> <ol> <li><strong>Chat App</strong>: Real-time messaging with Firebase</li> <li><strong>E-commerce App</strong>: Product catalog and cart</li> <li><strong>Fitness Tracker</strong>: Workout logging and statistics</li> <li><strong>Social Media App</strong>: Posts, likes, and comments</li> </ol> <h2 id="-best-practices"><a class="header" href="#-best-practices">🚀 Best Practices</a></h2> <h3 id="component-structure"><a class="header" href="#component-structure">Component Structure</a></h3> <pre><code class="language-javascript">// Good component structure import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react'; import { View, Text, StyleSheet } from 'react-native'; const MyComponent = ({ prop1, prop2 }) =&gt; { const [state, setState] = useState(null); useEffect(() =&gt; { // Side effects here }, []); return ( &lt;View style={styles.container}&gt; &lt;Text&gt;{prop1}&lt;/Text&gt; &lt;/View&gt; ); }; const styles = StyleSheet.create({ container: { // Styles here }, }); export default MyComponent; </code></pre> <h3 id="performance-tips"><a class="header" href="#performance-tips">Performance Tips</a></h3> <ul> <li>Use <code>FlatList</code> for long lists instead of <code>ScrollView</code> with <code>map</code></li> <li>Avoid unnecessary re-renders with <code>React.memo</code></li> <li>Use <code>useCallback</code> and <code>useMemo</code> for expensive operations</li> <li>Optimize images and use appropriate formats</li> <li>Test on real devices, not just simulators</li> </ul> <h2 id="-learning-path"><a class="header" href="#-learning-path">🎓 Learning Path</a></h2> <ol> <li><strong>Week 1</strong>: Setup and basic components</li> <li><strong>Week 2</strong>: Styling and layout</li> <li><strong>Week 3</strong>: Navigation and state management</li> <li><strong>Week 4</strong>: API integration and data handling</li> <li><strong>Week 5</strong>: Testing and debugging</li> <li><strong>Week 6</strong>: Performance optimization</li> <li><strong>Week 7</strong>: Advanced patterns and architecture</li> <li><strong>Week 8</strong>: Deployment and publishing</li> </ol> <h2 id="-resources"><a class="header" href="#-resources">🔗 Resources</a></h2> <h3 id="official-documentation"><a class="header" href="#official-documentation">Official Documentation</a></h3> <ul> <li><a href="https://reactnative.dev/">React Native Docs</a></li> <li><a href="https://docs.expo.dev/">Expo Documentation</a></li> <li><a href="https://github.com/react-native-community/">React Native Community</a></li> </ul> <h3 id="learning-resources"><a class="header" href="#learning-resources">Learning Resources</a></h3> <ul> <li><a href="https://reactnativeschool.com/">React Native School</a></li> <li><a href="https://reactnative.training/">React Native Training</a></li> <li><a href="https://www.youtube.com/results?search_query=react+native+tutorial">YouTube: React Native</a></li> </ul> <h3 id="community"><a class="header" href="#community">Community</a></h3> <ul> <li><a href="https://www.reddit.com/r/reactnative/">React Native Reddit</a></li> <li><a href="https://discord.gg/react-native">Discord: React Native</a></li> <li><a href="https://stackoverflow.com/questions/tagged/react-native">Stack Overflow</a></li> </ul> <hr> <p><strong>Ready to start building?</strong> Let’s dive into components and props in the next section! 🚀</p> <div style="break-before: page; page-break-before: always;"></div> <h1 id="components--props-in-react-native"><a class="header" href="#components--props-in-react-native">Components &amp; Props in React Native</a></h1> <p>Components are the building blocks of React Native applications. They encapsulate reusable pieces of UI and logic.</p> <h2 id="-understanding-components"><a class="header" href="#-understanding-components">🧩 Understanding Components</a></h2> <h3 id="what-is-a-component"><a class="header" href="#what-is-a-component">What is a Component?</a></h3> <p>A component is a self-contained, reusable piece of UI that can accept input (props) and manage its own state.</p> <pre><code class="language-javascript">import React from 'react'; import { View, Text, StyleSheet } from 'react-native'; // Functional Component const WelcomeCard = () =&gt; { return ( &lt;View style={styles.container}&gt; &lt;Text style={styles.title}&gt;Welcome!&lt;/Text&gt; &lt;/View&gt; ); }; const styles = StyleSheet.create({ container: { padding: 20, backgroundColor: '#f0f0f0', borderRadius: 8, }, title: { fontSize: 18, fontWeight: 'bold', }, }); export default WelcomeCard; </code></pre> <h2 id="-props-properties"><a class="header" href="#-props-properties">📦 Props (Properties)</a></h2> <p>Props are read-only attributes that pass data from parent to child components.</p> <h3 id="basic-props-usage"><a class="header" href="#basic-props-usage">Basic Props Usage</a></h3> <pre><code class="language-javascript">import React from 'react'; import { View, Text, StyleSheet } from 'react-native'; const UserCard = ({ name, email, avatar }) =&gt; { return ( &lt;View style={styles.card}&gt; &lt;Text style={styles.name}&gt;{name}&lt;/Text&gt; &lt;Text style={styles.email}&gt;{email}&lt;/Text&gt; &lt;/View&gt; ); }; // Parent Component const UserList = () =&gt; { const users = [ { name: 'John Doe', email: 'john@example.com' }, { name: 'Jane Smith', email: 'jane@example.com' }, ]; return ( &lt;View&gt; {users.map((user, index) =&gt; ( &lt;UserCard key={index} name={user.name} email={user.email} /&gt; ))} &lt;/View&gt; ); }; </code></pre> <h3 id="prop-types-and-validation"><a class="header" href="#prop-types-and-validation">Prop Types and Validation</a></h3> <pre><code class="language-javascript">import React from 'react'; import { View, Text, StyleSheet } from 'react-native'; import PropTypes from 'prop-types'; const Button = ({ title, onPress, disabled, color }) =&gt; { return ( &lt;TouchableOpacity style={[styles.button, { backgroundColor: color }]} onPress={onPress} disabled={disabled} &gt; &lt;Text style={styles.buttonText}&gt;{title}&lt;/Text&gt; &lt;/TouchableOpacity&gt; ); }; Button.propTypes = { title: PropTypes.string.isRequired, onPress: PropTypes.func.isRequired, disabled: PropTypes.bool, color: PropTypes.string, }; Button.defaultProps = { disabled: false, color: '#007AFF', }; </code></pre> <h2 id="-core-components"><a class="header" href="#-core-components">🎨 Core Components</a></h2> <h3 id="view"><a class="header" href="#view">View</a></h3> <p>The most fundamental component for building UI:</p> <pre><code class="language-javascript">import { View, StyleSheet } from 'react-native'; const Container = () =&gt; { return ( &lt;View style={styles.container}&gt; &lt;View style={styles.header} /&gt; &lt;View style={styles.content} /&gt; &lt;View style={styles.footer} /&gt; &lt;/View&gt; ); }; const styles = StyleSheet.create({ container: { flex: 1, }, header: { height: 60, backgroundColor: '#fff', }, content: { flex: 1, backgroundColor: '#f5f5f5', }, footer: { height: 50, backgroundColor: '#fff', }, }); </code></pre> <h3 id="text"><a class="header" href="#text">Text</a></h3> <p>For displaying text content:</p> <pre><code class="language-javascript">import { Text, StyleSheet } from 'react-native'; const TextExamples = () =&gt; { return ( &lt;View&gt; &lt;Text style={styles.title}&gt;Main Title&lt;/Text&gt; &lt;Text style={styles.subtitle}&gt;Subtitle Text&lt;/Text&gt; &lt;Text style={styles.body}&gt;Regular body text content&lt;/Text&gt; &lt;Text style={styles.caption}&gt;Small caption text&lt;/Text&gt; &lt;/View&gt; ); }; const styles = StyleSheet.create({ title: { fontSize: 24, fontWeight: 'bold', color: '#000', }, subtitle: { fontSize: 18, fontWeight: '600', color: '#333', }, body: { fontSize: 16, color: '#666', lineHeight: 24, }, caption: { fontSize: 12, color: '#999', }, }); </code></pre> <h3 id="image"><a class="header" href="#image">Image</a></h3> <p>For displaying images:</p> <pre><code class="language-javascript">import { Image, StyleSheet, View } from 'react-native'; const ImageExamples = () =&gt; { return ( &lt;View&gt; {/* Local Image */} &lt;Image source={require('./assets/logo.png')} style={styles.localImage} /&gt; {/* Network Image */} &lt;Image source={{ uri: 'https://example.com/image.jpg' }} style={styles.networkImage} /&gt; {/* Image with Placeholder */} &lt;Image source={require('./assets/profile.jpg')} style={styles.avatar} defaultSource={require('./assets/placeholder.png')} /&gt; &lt;/View&gt; ); }; </code></pre> <h3 id="touchableopacity"><a class="header" href="#touchableopacity">TouchableOpacity</a></h3> <p>For creating pressable elements:</p> <pre><code class="language-javascript">import { TouchableOpacity, Text, StyleSheet } from 'react-native'; const CustomButton = ({ title, onPress, variant }) =&gt; { const buttonStyle = variant === 'primary' ? styles.primaryButton : styles.secondaryButton; return ( &lt;TouchableOpacity style={buttonStyle} onPress={onPress}&gt; &lt;Text style={styles.buttonText}&gt;{title}&lt;/Text&gt; &lt;/TouchableOpacity&gt; ); }; </code></pre> <h2 id="-custom-components"><a class="header" href="#-custom-components">🏗️ Custom Components</a></h2> <h3 id="creating-reusable-components"><a class="header" href="#creating-reusable-components">Creating Reusable Components</a></h3> <pre><code class="language-javascript">import React from 'react'; import { View, Text, TouchableOpacity, StyleSheet } from 'react-native'; const Card = ({ children, title, onPress }) =&gt; { return ( &lt;TouchableOpacity style={styles.card} onPress={onPress}&gt; {title &amp;&amp; &lt;Text style={styles.title}&gt;{title}&lt;/Text&gt;} &lt;View style={styles.content}&gt; {children} &lt;/View&gt; &lt;/TouchableOpacity&gt; ); }; const InputField = ({ label, value, onChangeText, placeholder, secure }) =&gt; { return ( &lt;View style={styles.inputContainer}&gt; &lt;Text style={styles.label}&gt;{label}&lt;/Text&gt; &lt;TextInput style={styles.input} value={value} onChangeText={onChangeText} placeholder={placeholder} secureTextEntry={secure} /&gt; &lt;/View&gt; ); }; const LoadingSpinner = ({ size, color }) =&gt; { return ( &lt;ActivityIndicator size={size || 'large'} color={color || '#007AFF'} /&gt; ); }; </code></pre> <h2 id="-component-composition"><a class="header" href="#-component-composition">🔄 Component Composition</a></h2> <h3 id="building-complex-uis"><a class="header" href="#building-complex-uis">Building Complex UIs</a></h3> <pre><code class="language-javascript">import React from 'react'; import { View, ScrollView, StyleSheet } from 'react-native'; import Card from './Card'; import UserCard from './UserCard'; import LoadingSpinner from './LoadingSpinner'; const UserFeed = ({ users, loading, onUserPress }) =&gt; { if (loading) { return &lt;LoadingSpinner /&gt;; } return ( &lt;ScrollView style={styles.container}&gt; {users.map(user =&gt; ( &lt;Card key={user.id} onPress={() =&gt; onUserPress(user)}&gt; &lt;UserCard name={user.name} email={user.email} avatar={user.avatar} /&gt; &lt;/Card&gt; ))} &lt;/ScrollView&gt; ); }; </code></pre> <h2 id="-best-practices-1"><a class="header" href="#-best-practices-1">🎯 Best Practices</a></h2> <h3 id="1-single-responsibility"><a class="header" href="#1-single-responsibility">1. Single Responsibility</a></h3> <p>Each component should have one clear purpose:</p> <pre><code class="language-javascript">// Good: Single responsibility const Avatar = ({ source, size }) =&gt; ( &lt;Image source={source} style={[styles.avatar, { width: size, height: size }]} /&gt; ); // Bad: Multiple responsibilities const UserSection = ({ user, onEdit, onDelete, onMessage }) =&gt; { // Too many responsibilities in one component }; </code></pre> <h3 id="2-props-destructuring"><a class="header" href="#2-props-destructuring">2. Props Destructuring</a></h3> <p>Always destructure props for cleaner code:</p> <pre><code class="language-javascript">// Good const UserCard = ({ name, email, avatar }) =&gt; { return ( &lt;View&gt; &lt;Text&gt;{name}&lt;/Text&gt; &lt;Text&gt;{email}&lt;/Text&gt; &lt;/View&gt; ); }; // Avoid const UserCard = (props) =&gt; { return ( &lt;View&gt; &lt;Text&gt;{props.name}&lt;/Text&gt; &lt;Text&gt;{props.email}&lt;/Text&gt; &lt;/View&gt; ); }; </code></pre> <h3 id="3-default-props"><a class="header" href="#3-default-props">3. Default Props</a></h3> <p>Always provide sensible defaults:</p> <pre><code class="language-javascript">const Button = ({ title, onPress, disabled = false, variant = 'primary', size = 'medium' }) =&gt; { // Component implementation }; </code></pre> <h3 id="4-component-naming"><a class="header" href="#4-component-naming">4. Component Naming</a></h3> <p>Use descriptive, PascalCase names:</p> <pre><code class="language-javascript">// Good const UserProfileCard = () =&gt; {}; const NavigationHeader = () =&gt; {}; const SearchInputField = () =&gt; {}; // Avoid const Card = () =&gt; {}; // Too generic const Header = () =&gt; {}; // Too generic const Input = () =&gt; {}; // Too generic </code></pre> <h2 id="-testing-components"><a class="header" href="#-testing-components">🧪 Testing Components</a></h2> <h3 id="basic-component-testing"><a class="header" href="#basic-component-testing">Basic Component Testing</a></h3> <pre><code class="language-javascript">import React from 'react'; import { render, fireEvent } from '@testing-library/react-native'; import Button from '../Button'; describe('Button Component', () =&gt; { it('renders correctly with title', () =&gt; { const { getByText } = render( &lt;Button title="Press me" onPress={() =&gt; {}} /&gt; ); expect(getByText('Press me')).toBeTruthy(); }); it('calls onPress when pressed', () =&gt; { const mockOnPress = jest.fn(); const { getByText } = render( &lt;Button title="Press me" onPress={mockOnPress} /&gt; ); fireEvent.press(getByText('Press me')); expect(mockOnPress).toHaveBeenCalled(); }); }); </code></pre> <h2 id="-component-library"><a class="header" href="#-component-library">📚 Component Library</a></h2> <h3 id="building-a-component-library"><a class="header" href="#building-a-component-library">Building a Component Library</a></h3> <pre><code class="language-javascript">// components/index.js export { default as Button } from './Button'; export { default as Card } from './Card'; export { default as Input } from './Input'; export { default as Avatar } from './Avatar'; // Usage in other files import { Button, Card, Input } from '../components'; </code></pre> <h3 id="theme-integration"><a class="header" href="#theme-integration">Theme Integration</a></h3> <pre><code class="language-javascript">// theme.js export const colors = { primary: '#007AFF', secondary: '#5856D6', success: '#34C759', warning: '#FF9500', error: '#FF3B30', background: '#F2F2F7', surface: '#FFFFFF', text: '#000000', textSecondary: '#8E8E93', }; export const spacing = { xs: 4, sm: 8, md: 16, lg: 24, xl: 32, }; export const typography = { h1: { fontSize: 32, fontWeight: 'bold', }, h2: { fontSize: 24, fontWeight: 'bold', }, body: { fontSize: 16, fontWeight: 'normal', }, caption: { fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 'normal', }, }; // Themed Component const ThemedButton = ({ title, onPress }) =&gt; { return ( &lt;TouchableOpacity style={[styles.button, { backgroundColor: colors.primary }]} onPress={onPress} &gt; &lt;Text style={[styles.text, { color: colors.surface }]}&gt; {title} &lt;/Text&gt; &lt;/TouchableOpacity&gt; ); }; </code></pre> <hr> <p><strong>Next Up</strong>: Learn about navigation to connect your components into a complete app! 🚀</p> <div style="break-before: page; Persistence</a></h1> <div style="break-before: page; page-break-before: always;"></div> <h1 id="performance-optimization"><a class="header" href="#performance-optimization">Performance Optimization</a></h1> <div style="break-before: page; page-break-before: always;"></div> <h1 id="introduction-to-ai-development"><a class="header" href="#introduction-to-ai-development">Introduction to AI Development</a></h1> <p>Artificial Intelligence is no longer a futuristic concept - it’s a practical tool that developers can integrate into applications today. This section will teach you how to leverage AI, particularly ChatGPT and similar models, to build intelligent applications.</p> <h2 id="-what-is-ai-development"><a class="header" href="#-what-is-ai-development">🤖 What is AI Development?</a></h2> <p>AI Development involves:</p> <ul> <li><strong>Prompt Engineering</strong>: Crafting effective instructions for AI models</li> <li><strong>API Integration</strong>: Connecting your apps to AI services</li> <li><strong>AI-Powered Features</strong>: Building smart, responsive applications</li> <li><strong>Ethical AI</strong>: Understanding limitations and responsible usage</li> </ul> <h2 id="-why-learn-ai-development"><a class="header" href="#-why-learn-ai-development">🎯 Why Learn AI Development?</a></h2> <h3 id="market-demand"><a class="header" href="#market-demand">Market Demand</a></h3> <ul> <li>AI skills are among the highest-paid in tech</li> <li>Companies are actively seeking AI integration expertise</li> <li>Growing demand for AI-powered applications</li> </ul> <h3 id="career-benefits"><a class="header" href="#career-benefits">Career Benefits</a></h3> <ul> <li>Future-proof your development skills</li> <li>Command higher rates for AI projects</li> <li>Position yourself as a modern developer</li> </ul> <h3 id="innovation-opportunities"><a class="header" href="#innovation-opportunities">Innovation Opportunities</a></h3> <ul> <li>Build applications that were impossible before</li> <li>Create personalized user experiences</li> <li>Automate complex decision-making processes</li> </ul> <h2 id="-types-of-ai-well-cover"><a class="header" href="#-types-of-ai-well-cover">🧠 Types of AI We’ll Cover</a></h2> <h3 id="1-large-language-models-llms"><a class="header" href="#1-large-language-models-llms">1. Large Language Models (LLMs)</a></h3> <ul> <li><strong>ChatGPT/GPT-4</strong>: Text generation and understanding</li> <li><strong>Claude</strong>: Advanced reasoning and analysis</li> <li><strong>LLaMA</strong>: Open-source alternatives</li> </ul> <h3 id="2-ai-apis"><a class="header" href="#2-ai-apis">2. AI APIs</a></h3> <ul> <li><strong>OpenAI API</strong>: Access to GPT models</li> <li><strong>Google AI</strong>: Various AI services</li> <li><strong>Hugging Face</strong>: Open-source models</li> </ul> <h3 id="3-ai-integration-patterns"><a class="header" href="#3-ai-integration-patterns">3. AI Integration Patterns</a></h3> <ul> <li><strong>Chat Interfaces</strong>: Conversational applications</li> <li><strong>Content Generation</strong>: Automated writing and creation</li> <li><strong>Data Analysis</strong>: AI-powered insights</li> <li><strong>Image Generation</strong>: Visual AI applications</li> </ul> <h2 id="-core-concepts-1"><a class="header" href="#-core-concepts-1">🛠️ Core Concepts</a></h2> <h3 id="prompt-engineering"><a class="header" href="#prompt-engineering">Prompt Engineering</a></h3> <p>The art of writing effective instructions for AI models:</p> <pre><code class="language-javascript">// Basic prompt const basicPrompt = "Write a blog post about React Native"; // Advanced prompt with structure const advancedPrompt = ` Write a blog post about React Native with the following requirements: - Target audience: beginner developers - Length: 800-1000 words - Include code examples - Cover setup, basic components, and deployment - Use a friendly, encouraging tone `; // Prompt with examples (few-shot learning) const fewShotPrompt = ` Convert the following user requests into API calls: User: "Show me all users" API: GET /api/users User: "Create a new user named John" API: POST /api/users {"name": "John"} User: "Delete user with ID 123" API: DELETE /api/users/123 User: "${userRequest}" API: `; </code></pre> <h3 id="api-integration-1"><a class="header" href="#api-integration-1">API Integration</a></h3> <p>Connecting your applications to AI services:</p> <pre><code class="language-javascript">// OpenAI API integration import OpenAI from 'openai'; const openai = new OpenAI({ apiKey: process.env.OPENAI_API_KEY, }); const generateResponse = async (prompt) =&gt; { try { const response = await openai.chat.completions.create({ model: "gpt-4", messages: [{ role: "user", content: prompt }], max_tokens: 1000, temperature: 0.7, }); return response.choices[0].message.content; } catch (error) { console.error('AI API Error:', error); throw error; } }; </code></pre> <h3 id="error-handling"><a class="header" href="#error-handling">Error Handling</a></h3> <p>Robust error handling for AI services:</p> <pre><code class="language-javascript">const safeAICall = async (prompt, retries = 3) =&gt; { for (let i = 0; i &lt; retries; i++) { try { return await generateResponse(prompt); } catch (error) { if (i === retries - 1) { // Final attempt failed return "I'm having trouble connecting to my AI services. Please try again later."; } // Wait before retrying await new Promise(resolve =&gt; setTimeout(resolve, 1000 * (i + 1))); } } }; </code></pre> <h2 id="-ai-applications-youll-build"><a class="header" href="#-ai-applications-youll-build">🚀 AI Applications You’ll Build</a></h2> <h3 id="1-chatgpt-clone"><a class="header" href="#1-chatgpt-clone">1. id="development-tools"><a class="header" href="#development-tools">Development Tools</a></h3> <ul> <li><strong>Postman</strong>: API testing</li> <li><strong>VS Code Extensions</strong>: AI development helpers</li> <li><strong>Git</strong>: Version control for prompts</li> <li><strong>Environment Variables</strong>: Secure API key storage</li> </ul> <h3 id="monitoring-tools"><a class="header" href="#monitoring-tools">Monitoring Tools</a></h3> <ul> <li><strong>OpenAI Dashboard</strong>: Usage tracking</li> <li><strong>Custom Analytics</strong>: Response quality monitoring</li> <li><strong>Error Tracking</strong>: Issue identification</li> <li><strong>Cost Management</strong>: Budget control</li> </ul> <h3 id="testing-tools"><a class="header" Testing</strong>: Compare prompt variations</li> <li><strong>User Testing</strong>: Real-world feedback</li> </ul> <h2 id="-cost-management"><a class="header" href="#-cost-management">💰 Cost Management</a></h2> <h3 id="understanding-ai-api-costs"><a class="header" href="#understanding-ai-api-costs">Understanding AI API Costs</a></h3> <ul> <li><strong>Tokens</strong>: Basic unit of text processing</li> <li><strong>Models</strong>: Different pricing tiers</li> <li><strong>Usage</strong>: Pay-per-request vs. subscriptions</li> <li><strong>Optimization</strong>: Reducing unnecessary calls</li> </ul> <h3 id="cost-optimization-strategies"><a class="header" href="#cost-optimization-strategies">Cost Optimization Strategies</a></h3> <pre><code class="language-javascript">// Caching AI responses const cache = new Map(); const getCachedResponse = async (prompt) =&gt; { const cacheKey = prompt.trim().toLowerCase(); if (cache.has(cacheKey)) { return cache.get(cacheKey); } const response = await generateResponse(prompt); cache.set(cacheKey, response); return response; }; // Batch processing const batchProcess = async (prompts) =&gt; { const responses = await Promise.all( prompts.map(prompt =&gt; generateResponse(prompt)) ); return responses; }; </code></pre> <h2 id="-security-considerations"><a class="header" href="#-security-considerations">🛡️ Security Considerations</a></h2> <h3 id="api-key-protection"><a class="header" href="#api-key-protection">API Key Protection</a></h3> <pre><code class="language-javascript">// Never hardcode API keys // ❌ BAD const openai = new OpenAI({ apiKey: "sk-..." }); // ✅ GOOD const openai = new OpenAI({ apiKey: process.env.OPENAI_API_KEY }); // ✅ EVEN BETTER (with validation) const apiKey = process.env.OPENAI_API_KEY; if (!apiKey) { throw new Error('OpenAI API key not configured'); } const openai = new OpenAI({ apiKey }); </code></pre> <h3 id="data-privacy"><a class="header" href="#data-privacy">Data Privacy</a></h3> <ul> <li><strong>PII Detection</strong>: Identify and protect personal information</li> <li><strong>Data Sanitization</strong>: Clean inputs before sending to AI</li> <li><strong>User Consent</strong>: Inform users about AI usage</li> <li><strong>Compliance</strong>: Follow GDPR and other regulations</li> </ul> <h2 id="-learning-path-1"><a class="header" section! 🚀</p> <div style="break-before: page; page-break-before: always;"></div> <h1 id="prompt-engineering-1"><a class="header" href="#prompt-engineering-1">Prompt Engineering</a></h1> <h2 id="what-is-prompt-engineering"><a class="header" href="#what-is-prompt-engineering">What is Prompt Engineering?</a></h2> <p>Prompt engineering is the art and science of designing effective instructions (prompts) to guide AI models like ChatGPT to produce desired outputs. It’s a critical skill for modern developers working with AI.</p> <h2 id="example"><a class="header" href="#example">Example</a></h2> <h3 id="basic-vs-advanced-prompting"><a class="header" href="#basic-vs-advanced-prompting">Basic vs. Advanced Prompting</a></h3> <pre><code class="language-javascript">// Basic prompt (limited results) const basicPrompt = "Write about React Native"; // Advanced prompt (specific, structured results) const advancedPrompt = ` Write a comprehensive guide about React Native development with the following requirements: TARGET AUDIENCE: Intermediate developers familiar with JavaScript LENGTH: 1500-2000 words STRUCTURE: 1. Introduction to React Native 2. Core Components and Concepts 3. Navigation Patterns 4. State Management Options 5. Performance Optimization 6. Testing Strategies 7. Deployment Process STYLE: Professional yet approachable INCLUDE: Code examples for each section AVOID: Basic JavaScript explanations FOCUS: Practical, production-ready advice Please provide detailed explanations with working code examples. `; </code></pre> <h3 id="prompt-template-system"><a class="header" href="#prompt-template-system">Prompt Template System</a></h3> <pre><code class="language-javascript">// Prompt templates for consistency class PromptTemplate { constructor(template, variables = {}) { this.template = template; this.variables = variables; } generate(variables) { let prompt = this.template; Object.entries({ ...this.variables, ...variables }).forEach(([key, value]) =&gt; { prompt = prompt.replace(new RegExp(`{{${key}}}`, 'g'), value); }); return prompt; } } // Blog post template const blogPostTemplate = new PromptTemplate(` Write a {{tone}} blog post about {{topic}} for {{audience}}. Requirements: - Length: {{length}} words - Include {{codeExamples}} code examples - Focus on {{focus}} - Style: {{style}} Structure: {{structure}} Please ensure the content is {{quality}} and {{actionable}}. `); // Usage const blogPrompt = blogPostTemplate.generate({ topic: "React Native performance optimization", audience: "mobile developers", tone: "technical", length: "1200", codeExamples: "3-5", focus: "practical optimization techniques", style: "clear and concise", structure: ` 1. Performance bottlenecks identification 2. Memory optimization 3. Rendering optimization 4. Network optimization 5. Testing and monitoring `, quality: "production-ready", actionable: "includes actionable tips" }); </code></pre> <h2 id="real-use-case"><a class="header" href="#real-use-case">Real Use Case</a></h2> <h3 id="customer-support-ai-prompt"><a class="header" href="#customer-support-ai-prompt">Customer Support AI Prompt</a></h3> <p>Companies like <strong>Stripe</strong> and <strong>Shopify</strong> use sophisticated prompt engineering for customer support:</p> <pre><code class="language-javascript">// Customer support prompt template const customerSupportPrompt = ` You are a helpful customer support agent for {{companyName}}. Your role: {{agentRole}} Company: {{companyDescription}} Product: {{productDescription}} Guidelines: - Always be empathetic and professional - Provide accurate, helpful information - If you don't know something, admit it and escalate - Follow company policies and tone - Aim for first-contact resolution when possible Customer Query: {{customerQuery}} Customer History: {{customerHistory}} Previous Interactions: {{previousInteractions}} Please provide a response that: 1. Acknowledges the customer's issue 2. Shows understanding of their situation 3. Provides a clear solution or next steps 4. Maintains the company's brand voice 5. Includes any relevant resources Response Format: [Greeting] [Empathy statement] [Solution/Action] [Additional help] [Closing] `; // Implementation class CustomerSupportAI { constructor() { this.promptTemplate = customerSupportPrompt; } async generateResponse(customerData) { const prompt = this.promptTemplate.generate({ companyName: "TechCorp", agentRole: "Senior Support Specialist", companyDescription: "Leading SaaS platform for project management", productDescription: "Cloud-based project collaboration tools", customerQuery: customerData.query, customerHistory: customerData.history, previousInteractions: customerData.interactions }); return await this.callAI(prompt); } } </code></pre> <h2 id="pro-tip"><a class="header" href="#pro-tip">Pro Tip</a></h2> <p><strong>Use Chain-of-Thought Prompting for Complex Problems</strong></p> <pre><code class="language-javascript">// Chain-of-thought prompting for debugging const debuggingPrompt = ` I need help debugging a React Native issue. Let me think through this step by step. PROBLEM: {{problemDescription}} ERROR MESSAGE: {{errorMessage}} CODE SNIPPET: {{codeSnippet}} EXPECTED BEHAVIOR: {{expectedBehavior}} ACTUAL BEHAVIOR: {{actualBehavior}} Let's analyze this systematically: 1. First, let's identify the type of error: - Is it a syntax error? - Is it a runtime error? - Is it a logic error? - Is it a platform-specific issue? 2. Next, let's examine the error message: - What does the error message tell us? - Where in the code is the error occurring? - What conditions trigger this error? 3. Then, let's review the code: - Are there any obvious syntax issues? - Are we using APIs correctly? - Are there any missing dependencies or imports? 4. Consider the context: - What platform (iOS/Android) is this on? - What React Native version? - What device/emulator is being used? 5. Potential solutions: - Based on the analysis, what are the most likely fixes? - What debugging steps should we try? - What additional information would be helpful? Please walk through this analysis and provide specific, actionable debugging steps. `; // Usage for complex debugging const debugPrompt = debuggingPrompt.generate({ problemDescription: "App crashes when navigating to second screen", errorMessage: "TypeError: undefined is not an object (evaluating 'navigation.navigate')", codeSnippet: ` const HomeScreen = ({ navigation }) =&gt; { return ( &lt;View&gt; &lt;Button title="Go to Details" onPress={() =&gt; navigation.navigate('Details')} /&gt; &lt;/View&gt; ); }; `, expectedBehavior: "Navigate to Details screen when button is pressed", actualBehavior: "App crashes with TypeError" }); </code></pre> <h2 id="exercise"><a class="header" href="#exercise">Exercise</a></h2> <p><strong>Build a Smart Code Review Assistant</strong></p> <p>Create a prompt engineering system that provides intelligent code reviews:</p> <pre><code class="language-javascript">// Code review prompt template const codeReviewTemplate = new PromptTemplate(` You are an expert {{language}} developer conducting a code review. AI Integration</p> <div style="break-before: page; page-break-before: always;"></div> <h1 id="ai-integration"><a class="header" href="#ai-integration">AI Integration</a></h1> <h2 id="what-is-ai-integration"><a class="header" href="#what-is-ai-integration">What is AI Integration?</a></h2> <p>AI integration is the process of incorporating artificial intelligence capabilities into software applications to enhance functionality, automate processes, and provide intelligent user experiences. It transforms traditional applications into smart systems that can learn, predict, and adapt.</p> <h2 id="example-1"><a class="header" href="#example-1">Example</a></h2> <h3 id="openai-api-integration-in-nodejs"><a class="header" href="#openai-api-integration-in-nodejs">OpenAI API Integration in Node.js</a></h3> <pre><code class="language-javascript">// services/aiService.js const OpenAI = require('openai'); class AIService { constructor() { this.openai = new OpenAI({ apiKey: process.env.OPENAI_API_KEY, }); } async generateResponse(prompt, options = {}) { try { const completion = await this.openai.chat.completions.create({ model: options.model || 'gpt-3.5-turbo', messages: [ { role: 'system', content: 'You are a helpful assistant.' }, { role: 'user', content: prompt } ], max_tokens: options.maxTokens || 1000, temperature: options.temperature || 0.7, }); return completion.choices[0].message.content; } catch (error) { console.error('AI Service Error:', error); throw new Error('Failed to generate AI response'); } } async analyzeText(text) { const prompt = `Analyze this text for sentiment, key topics, and insights: "${text}"`; return this.generateResponse(prompt); } } module.exports = AIService; </code></pre> <h3 id="react-native-ai-integration"><a class="header" href="#react-native-ai-integration">React Native AI Integration</a></h3> <pre><code class="language-javascript">// hooks/useAI.js import { useState, useCallback } from 'react'; import AIService from '../services/aiService'; export const useAI = () =&gt; { const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false); const [response, setResponse] = useState(''); const [error, setError] = useState(null); const generateResponse = useCallback(async (prompt, options) =&gt; { setLoading(true); setError(null); try { const aiService = new AIService(); const result = await aiService.generateResponse(prompt, options); setResponse(result); } catch (err) { setError(err.message); } finally { setLoading(false); } }, []); return { generateResponse, response, loading, error }; }; </code></pre> <h2 id="real-use-case-1"><a class="header" href="#real-use-case-1">Real Use Case</a></h2> <h3 id="customer-support-chatbot"><a class="header" href="#customer-support-chatbot">Customer Support Chatbot</a></h3> <p>Companies like <strong>Intercom</strong> and <strong>Zendesk</strong> use AI integration to power customer support:</p> <pre><code class="language-javascript">// components/AIChatbot.js import React, { useState } from 'react'; import { useAI } from '../hooks/useAI'; const AIChatbot = () =&gt; { const [messages, setMessages] = useState([]); const [input, setInput] = useState(''); const { generateResponse, loading } = useAI(); const sendMessage = async () =&gt; { if (!input.trim()) return; const userMessage = { role: 'user', content: input }; setMessages(prev =&gt; [...prev, userMessage]); // Generate AI response const aiPrompt = `Customer asked: "${input}". Provide helpful customer support response.`; const aiResponse = await generateResponse(aiPrompt); const botMessage = { role: 'assistant', content: aiResponse }; setMessages(prev =&gt; [...prev, botMessage]); setInput(''); }; return ( &lt;div className="chatbot"&gt; &lt;div className="messages"&gt; {messages.map((msg, i) =&gt; ( &lt;div key={i} className={`message ${msg.role}`}&gt; {msg.content} &lt;/div&gt; ))} &lt;/div&gt; &lt;div className="input-area"&gt; &lt;input value={input} onChange={(e) =&gt; setInput(e.target.value)} placeholder="Ask me anything..." onKeyPress={(e) =&gt; e.key === 'Enter' &amp;&amp; sendMessage()} /&gt; &lt;button onClick={sendMessage} disabled={loading}&gt; {loading ? 'Thinking...' : 'Send'} &lt;/button&gt; &lt;/div&gt; &lt;/div&gt; ); }; </code></pre> <h2 id="pro-tip-1"><a class="header" href="#pro-tip-1">Pro Tip</a></h2> <p><strong>Implement Rate Limiting and Caching</strong></p> <pre><code class="language-javascript">// utils/aiCache.js class AICache { constructor(maxSize = 100) { this.cache = new Map(); this.maxSize = maxSize; } get(key) { if (this.cache.has(key)) { // Move to end (LRU) const value = this.cache.get(key); this.cache.delete(key); this.cache.set(key, value); return value; } return null; } set(key, value) { if (this.cache.size &gt;= this.maxSize) { // Remove oldest entry const firstKey = this.cache.keys().next().value; this.cache.delete(firstKey); } this.cache.set(key, value); } } // Enhanced AI Service with caching class EnhancedAIService extends AIService { constructor() { super(); this.cache = new AICache(); this.rateLimiter = new Map(); // Simple rate limiting } async generateResponse(prompt, options = {}) { const cacheKey = `${prompt}_${JSON.stringify(options)}`; // Check cache first const cached = this.cache.get(cacheKey); if (cached) { return cached; } // Simple rate limiting const clientId = options.clientId || 'default'; const now = Date.now(); const lastRequest = this.rateLimiter.get(clientId) || 0; if (now - lastRequest &lt; 1000) { // 1 second between requests throw new Error('Rate limit exceeded. Please wait.'); } this.rateLimiter.set(clientId, now); // Generate response const response = await super.generateResponse(prompt, options); // Cache the result this.cache.set(cacheKey, response); return response; } } </code></pre> <h2 id="exercise-1"><a class="header" href="#exercise-1">Exercise</a></h2> <p><strong>Build a Simple AI Content Generator</strong></p> <p>Create a React Native component that uses AI to generate blog post titles based on a topic:</p> <pre><code class="language-javascript">// components/AIContentGenerator.js import React, { useState } from 'react'; import { useAI } from '../hooks/useAI'; const AIContentGenerator = () =&gt; { const [topic, setTopic] = useState(''); const [titles, setTitles] = useState([]); const { generateResponse, loading } = useAI(); const generateTitles = async () =&gt; { if (!topic.trim()) return; const prompt = `Generate 5 catchy blog post titles about: "${topic}". Return as a numbered list.`; try { const response = await generateResponse(prompt); // Parse the numbered list const titleList = response .split('\n') .filter(line =&gt; line.match(/^\d+\./)) .map(line =&gt; line.replace(/^\d+\.\s*/, '').trim()); setTitles(titleList); } catch (error) { console.error('Failed to generate titles:', error); } }; return ( &lt;div style={{ padding: 20 }}&gt; &lt;h2&gt;AI Blog Title Generator&lt;/h2&gt; &lt;input value={topic} onChange={(e) =&gt; setTopic(e.target.value)} placeholder="Enter a topic..." style={{ width: '100%', padding: 10, marginBottom: 10, border: '1px solid #ccc', borderRadius: 5 }} /&gt; &lt;button onClick={generateTitles} disabled={loading || !topic.trim()} style={{ padding: 10, backgroundColor: loading ? '#ccc' : '#007bff', color: 'white', border: 'none', borderRadius: 5, cursor: loading ? 'not-allowed' : 'pointer' }} &gt; {loading ? 'Generating...' : 'Generate Titles'} &lt;/button&gt; {titles.length &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; ( &lt;div style={{ marginTop: 20 }}&gt; &lt;h3&gt;Generated Titles:&lt;/h3&gt; {titles.map((title, i) =&gt; ( &lt;div key={i} style={{ padding: 10, backgroundColor: '#f8f9fa', marginBottom: 5, borderRadius: 5 }}&gt; {title} &lt;/div&gt; ))} &lt;/div&gt; )} &lt;/div&gt; ); }; export default AIContentGenerator; </code></pre> <p><strong>Your Tasks:</strong></p> <ol> <li>Implement the AI content generator component</li> <li>Add error handling for API failures</li> <li>Create a loading indicator during AI generation</li> <li>Add a feature to save favorite titles</li> <li>Implement character limit for the topic input</li> </ol> <p>This exercise teaches you practical AI integration, error handling, and user experience considerations when working with AI APIs.</p> <hr> <p><strong>Next Up</strong>: Learn about building a complete ChatGPT Clone! ChatGPT Clone</p> <div style="break-before: page; page-break-before: always;"></div> <h1 id="build-chatgpt-clone"><a class="header" href="#build-chatgpt-clone">Build: ChatGPT Clone</a></h1> <h2 id="what-is-it"><a class="header" href="#what-is-it">What is it?</a></h2> <p>A ChatGPT Clone is a conversational AI application that mimics the functionality of OpenAI’s ChatGPT interface. It provides real-time conversations with AI models, maintains conversation history, and offers a user-friendly chat interface.</p> <h2 id="example-2"><a class="header" href="#example-2">Example</a></h2> <h3 id="core-chat-component"><a class="header" href="#core-chat-component">Core Chat Component</a></h3> <pre><code class="language-javascript">// components/ChatInterface.js import React, { useState, useRef, useEffect } from 'react'; import { View, Text, TextInput, TouchableOpacity, FlatList, KeyboardAvoidingView, Platform } from 'react-native'; import { useAI } from '../hooks/useAI'; import MessageBubble from './MessageBubble'; import TypingIndicator from './TypingIndicator'; const ChatInterface = ({ systemPrompt = "You are a helpful assistant." }) =&gt; { const [messages, setMessages] = useState([]); const [inputText, setInputText] = useState(''); const [isTyping, setIsTyping] = useState(false); const flatListRef = useRef(null); const { generateResponse, loading } = useAI(); useEffect(() =&gt; { // Add welcome message setMessages([{ id: '1', role: 'assistant', content: 'Hello! How can I help you today?', timestamp: new Date() }]); }, []); const sendMessage = async () =&gt; { if (!inputText.trim() || loading) return; const userMessage = { id: Date.now().toString(), role: 'user', content: inputText.trim(), timestamp: new Date() }; setMessages(prev =&gt; [...prev, userMessage]); setInputText(''); setIsTyping(true); try { // Build conversation context const conversationHistory = messages .slice(-10) // Keep last 10 messages for context .map(msg =&gt; `${msg.role}: ${msg.content}`) .join('\n'); const prompt = `${systemPrompt}\n\nConversation History:\n${conversationHistory}\n\nuser: ${inputText}\nassistant:`; const response = await generateResponse(prompt, { model: 'gpt-3.5-turbo', maxTokens: 1000, temperature: 0.7 }); const assistantMessage = { id: (Date.now() + 1).toString(), role: 'assistant', content: response, timestamp: new Date() }; setMessages(prev =&gt; [...prev, assistantMessage]); } catch (error) { const errorMessage = { id: (Date.now() + 1).toString(), role: 'assistant', content: 'Sorry, I encountered an error. Please try again.', timestamp: new Date(), isError: true }; setMessages(prev =&gt; [...prev, errorMessage]); } finally { setIsTyping(false); } }; const renderMessage = ({ item }) =&gt; ( &lt;MessageBubble message={item} isUser={item.role === 'user'} /&gt; ); return ( &lt;KeyboardAvoidingView style={{ flex: 1 }} behavior={Platform.OS === 'ios' ? 'padding' : 'height'} &gt; &lt;View style={{ flex: 1 }}&gt; &lt;FlatList ref={flatListRef} data={messages} renderItem={renderMessage} keyExtractor={item =&gt; item.id} style={{ flex: 1, padding: 16 }} onContentSizeChange={() =&gt; { flatListRef.current?.scrollToEnd({ animated: true }); }} /&gt; {isTyping &amp;&amp; &lt;TypingIndicator /&gt;} &lt;View style={{ flexDirection: 'row', padding: 16, borderTopWidth: 1, borderTopColor: '#e0e0e0' }}&gt; &lt;TextInput style={{ flex: 1, borderWidth: 1, borderColor: '#ddd', borderRadius: 20, paddingHorizontal: 16, paddingVertical: 8, marginRight: 8, maxHeight: 100 }} value={inputText} onChangeText={setInputText} placeholder="Type your message..." multiline editable={!loading} /&gt; &lt;TouchableOpacity style={{ backgroundColor: '#007AFF', borderRadius: 20, paddingHorizontal: 20, paddingVertical: 8, justifyContent: 'center', opacity: (inputText.trim() &amp;&amp; !loading) ? 1 : 0.5 }} onPress={sendMessage} disabled={!inputText.trim() || loading} &gt; &lt;Text style={{ color: 'white', fontWeight: 'bold' }}&gt; {loading ? '...' : 'Send'} &lt;/Text&gt; &lt;/TouchableOpacity&gt; &lt;/View&gt; &lt;/View&gt; &lt;/KeyboardAvoidingView&gt; ); }; export default ChatInterface; </code></pre> <h3 id="message-bubble-component"><a class="header" href="#message-bubble-component">Message Bubble Component</a></h3> <pre><code class="language-javascript">// components/MessageBubble.js import React from 'react'; import { View, Text, StyleSheet } from 'react-native'; const MessageBubble = ({ message, isUser }) =&gt; { return ( &lt;View style={[ styles.messageContainer, isUser ? styles.userContainer : styles.assistantContainer ]}&gt; &lt;View style={[ styles.bubble, isUser ? styles.userBubble : styles.assistantBubble, message.isError &amp;&amp; styles.errorBubble ]}&gt; &lt;Text style={[ styles.messageText, isUser ? styles.userText : styles.assistantText ]}&gt; {message.content} &lt;/Text&gt; &lt;/View&gt; &lt;Text style={styles.timestamp}&gt; {message.timestamp.toLocaleTimeString()} &lt;/Text&gt; &lt;/View&gt; ); }; const styles = StyleSheet.create({ messageContainer: { marginVertical: 4, alignItems: 'flex-start' }, userContainer: { alignItems: 'flex-end' }, assistantContainer: { alignItems: 'flex-start' }, bubble: { maxWidth: '80%', padding: 12, borderRadius: 18, marginHorizontal: 8 }, userBubble: { backgroundColor: '#007AFF' }, assistantBubble: { backgroundColor: '#f0f0f0' }, errorBubble: { backgroundColor: '#ffebee' }, messageText: { fontSize: 16, lineHeight: 20 }, userText: { color: 'white' }, assistantText: { color: '#333' }, timestamp: { fontSize: 12, color: '#999', marginTop: 4, marginHorizontal: 12 } }); export default MessageBubble; </code></pre> <h2 id="real-use-case-2"><a class="header" href="#real-use-case-2">Real Use Case</a></h2> <h3 id="customer-service-chatbot"><a class="header" href="#customer-service-chatbot">Customer Service Chatbot</a></h3> <p><strong>Zendesk</strong> and <strong>Intercom</strong> use similar chat interfaces for customer support:</p> <pre><code class="language-javascript">// services/CustomerServiceBot.js class CustomerServiceBot { constructor() { this.systemPrompt = ` You are a helpful customer service representative for TechCorp. Company Information: - We sell software development tools - Pricing: Basic $29/month, Pro $99/month, Enterprise custom - Support: Email support for all, priority support for Pro+ - Refund policy: 30-day money-back guarantee Guidelines: - Always be empathetic and professional - Provide accurate information about our products - If you don't know something, admit it and offer to escalate - Try to resolve issues on first contact - Keep responses concise but helpful Common Issues: 1. Login problems: Check email/password, suggest password reset 2. Billing questions: Direct to billing@techcorp.com 3. Technical issues: Ask for error messages and system info 4. Feature requests: Thank customer and add to feature request queue `; } async handleCustomerMessage(message, customerContext) { const contextPrompt = ` Customer Context: - Plan: ${customerContext.plan || 'Unknown'} - Account age: ${customerContext.accountAge || 'Unknown'} - Previous issues: ${customerContext.previousIssues || 'None'} Current Message: ${message} Please provide a helpful response following our guidelines. `; return await this.generateResponse(contextPrompt); } async generateResponse(prompt) { // AI API call implementation return "AI response would go here"; } } </code></pre> <h2 id="pro-tip-2"><a class="header" href="#pro-tip-2">Pro Tip</a></h2> <p><strong>Implement Conversation Persistence and Context Management</strong></p> <pre><code class="language-javascript">// utils/ConversationManager.js class ConversationManager { constructor(maxMessages = 50) { this.maxMessages = maxMessages; this.conversations = new Map(); } // Save conversation to local storage async saveConversation(userId, messages) { try { const conversationData = { userId, messages: messages.slice(-this.maxMessages), // Keep only recent messages lastUpdated: new Date().toISOString() }; // Save to AsyncStorage (React Native) or localStorage (Web) if (typeof window !== 'undefined') { localStorage.setItem(`chat_${userId}`, JSON.stringify(conversationData)); } else { // React Native AsyncStorage implementation const AsyncStorage = require('@react-native-async-storage/async-storage').default; await AsyncStorage.setItem(`chat_${userId}`, JSON.stringify(conversationData)); } } catch (error) { console.error('Failed to save conversation:', error); } } // Load conversation from storage async loadConversation(userId) { try { let conversationData; if (typeof window !== 'undefined') { const stored = localStorage.getItem(`chat_${userId}`); conversationData = stored ? JSON.parse(stored) : null; } else { const AsyncStorage = require('@react-native-async-storage/async-storage').default; const stored = await AsyncStorage.getItem(`chat_${userId}`); conversationData = stored ? JSON.parse(stored) : null; } return conversationData?.messages || []; } catch (error) { console.error('Failed to load conversation:', error); return []; } } // Clear conversation history async clearConversation(userId) { try { if (typeof window !== 'undefined') { localStorage.removeItem(`chat_${userId}`); } else { const AsyncStorage = require('@react-native-async-storage/async-storage').default; await AsyncStorage.removeItem(`chat_${userId}`); } } catch (error) { console.error('Failed to clear conversation:', error); } } // Build context for AI model buildContext(messages, systemPrompt, maxTokens = 2000) { let context = systemPrompt + '\n\n'; let tokenCount = this.estimateTokens(context); // Add messages in reverse order, staying within token limit for (let i = messages.length - 1; i &gt;= 0; i--) { const message = messages[i]; const messageText = `${message.role}: ${message.content}\n`; const messageTokens = this.estimateTokens(messageText); if (tokenCount + messageTokens &gt; maxTokens) { break; } context = messageText + context; tokenCount += messageTokens; } return context; } // Simple token estimation (rough approximation) estimateTokens(text) { return Math.ceil(text.length / 4); } } </code></pre> <h2 id="exercise-2"><a class="header" href="#exercise-2">Exercise</a></h2> <p><strong>Build a Complete ChatGPT Clone with Advanced Features</strong></p> <p>Create a full-featured chat application with the following components:</p> <pre><code class="language-javascript">// App.js - Main application import React, { useState } from 'react'; setCurrentScreen('settings')} &gt; &lt;Text style={styles.settingsButtonText}&gt;Settings&lt;/Text&gt; &lt;/TouchableOpacity&gt; )} &lt;/View&gt; &lt;View style={styles.content}&gt; {renderScreen()} &lt;/View&gt; &lt;/SafeAreaView&gt; ); }; const styles = StyleSheet.create({ container: { flex: 1, backgroundColor: '#fff' }, header: { flexDirection: 'row', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center', padding: 16, borderBottomWidth: 1, borderBottomColor: '#e0e0e0' }, title: { fontSize: 20, fontWeight: 'bold', color: '#333' }, settingsButton: { paddingHorizontal: 12, paddingVertical: 6, backgroundColor: '#007AFF', borderRadius: 16 }, settingsButtonText: { color: 'white', fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 'bold' }, content: { flex: 1 } });
